For restoring fiscal sustainability and strengthening fiscal discipline, very ambitious, primarily revenue-based fiscal consolidation accompanied by fiscal institutional reforms and cost recovery-based energy pricing will be introduced by this Agreement. Another important element is a strong social safety net to protect the most vulnerable. We know that we cannot wait till full economic recovery to provide relief to the poorest sector of the population. An allocation not exceeding Rs. 187 billion will be made available to strengthen the existing cash transfer programmes relating to Samurdhi, people with disabilities, the elderly citizens and patients suffering from Chronic Kidney Disease in 2023. Also under this programme, the fuel prices will be determined on the 2018 price formula and will be adjusted once a month to ensure cost recovery. The electricity tariff will be adjusted every year in January and July to reflect the cost. An independent National Debt Management Agency will be set up according to global best practices. I wanted to mention all these elements to show that this very comprehensive programme covers all aspects of our reeling economy.

One of the most popular criticisms put forward by the Opposition in this Debate is that the Government plans to privatize profit-making State-owned enterprises in line with the IMF Agreement. I must say that those arguments and criticisms are obsolete or archaic and are far away from the modern global concepts of privatization and competition. Government cannot do business; businesses have to be run by businessmen. Governments are run by politicians, not by businessmen. Businesses are run by businessmen. Government uses people’s money, but businessmen risk their own money. So, they are careful.

1071 1072

[ගරු නීතිඥ පසන්ත මපමංණ්ඩමය බතම]

2023 මර්තු 22

But, when it comes to businesses run by the Government, nobody is responsible or accountable for the money used. We have been just running those enterprises. That is what we have been doing. We have been running those enterprises - they have been making profit - but that does not mean those have been running effectively and efficiently, that they have been making enough profit, but they should have.

State-owned enterprises tend to be monopolies or restrict competition from the private sector. The Government cannot boost overall employment by hiring workers for the State sector. State-owned enterprises do enjoy hidden subsidies in various forms including preferential borrowing costs, lower rents or taxes. Therefore, Sir, time has come for us to critically look at whether those profit-making SOEs are actually, in real terms making profit. So, it is in that context that divestment of State assets comes in as part of the Government’s restructuring process of state sector enterprises. Therefore, we need to strongly support President Ranil Wickremesinghe’s State sector restructuring plans to reduce burden on the people. When there is an economic crisis, you need to make sacrifices to safeguard the country. Therefore, it is imperative that we sell some of those ventures to protect the economy. You might have to amputate your leg to save your life; it is an existential choice.

Sir, I wish to conclude by reiterating the fact that the business of the Government is not to do business, but to provide a conducive environment for its people and investors to carry out their activities freely and competitively subject to a strong regulatory mechanism to ensure maximum economic and social benefit to the people and the country.

Let us learn from the successful models of neighbouring countries like Singapore, Malaysia, India et cetera, who embraced the open economy much later than Sri Lanka did. Let us make patriotic decisions not only by heart, but also from the brain. Sri Lanka is clearly at the crossroads and let us make the right and futuristic choices for the sake of our motherland and for our future generations.

Thank you. ගු නිවයෝනය කථානායකතුමා (மொண்புமிகு பிரதிச் சபொநொயகர் அவர்கள்) (The Hon. Deputy Speaker) ජමතයන්තය ූලකය අයමුදක ස ඟ ශ්‍රී කා ම යජ ඇති ය ගන්්ම කද ගිවිසු සපතංන්ධප ගරු ජ්මධිපතිතු ම විසින් ශපත ගරු සභමපට ය් කද ප්‍ර ම පිළිංඳ අද දි් ආයපතභ ළ සභමප ස් තං් අපසාථමශේ විපමද 2023 මර්තු ස 23පකනි දි් තපුවයට ක පකපක කවී පිණිස ස් තංනු කං් ංප දන්පනු ක ක කශතමි.

එකල්හි වේලාව අ.භා. 5.30 වූවයන් ගු නිවයෝනය කථානායකතුමා විිංන් ප්‍රශ්නය වන්විමසා පාර්ලිවම්න්තුව කල් තබන ලදී.

පාර්ලිවම්න්තුව ඊ අනුකූලව 2023 මාර්තු 23වන බ්‍රහස්පතින්දා පූ.භා. 9.30 වන වත කල් ගිවේ ය.

அப்தபொழுது, பி.ப. 5.30 மைியொகிவிடசவ மொண்புமிகு பிரதிச் சபொநொயகர் அவர்கள் வினொ விடுக்கொமசலசய பொரொளுமன்றத்மத ஒத்திமவத்தொர்.

அதன்படி பொரொளுமன்றம், 2023 மொர்ச் 23, வியொழக்கிழமம மு.ப. 9.30 மைிவமர ஒத்திமவக்கப்பட்டது.

It being 5.30 p.m., THE HON. DEPUTY SPEAKER adjourned Parliament without Question put.

Parliament adjourned accordingly until 9.30 a.m. on Thursday, 23rd March, 2023.

1073 1074

සැ.යු.

ශ පමර්තමශේ අපසම් මුද්‍රට සඳබම සාපකී ථමපක නිපකයදි ළ යුතු තකන් දක්පනු රිසි න්ත්‍රීන් මින් පිටපතක් ශග්

නිපකයදි ළ යුතු ආ මය එ ර පකබකදිලිප කව ණු ශ ්ට, පිටපත කකබී ශදසති ක් ශ්්ික් පම

හැන්සාඩ් සාසා මය ශපත කකශං් ශසේ එවි යුතු .

குறிப்பு

உறுப்பினர் தமது உமரயின் இறுதிப் பதிப்பிற் தசய்யவிரும்பும் பிமழ திருத்தங்கமள தமது பிரதியில் ததளிவொகக் குறித்து

அதமனப் பிமழ திருத்தப்படொத பிரதி கிமடத்த இரு வொரங்களுள் ஹன்சொட் பதிப்பொசிொியருக்கு அனுப்புதல் சவண்டும்.

Corrections which Members suggest for the Final Print of their speeches should be clearly marked in their copy and

sent to the Editor of HANSARD within two weeks of receipt of the uncorrected copy.

හැන්සාඩ් වාර්තා වක්මඹ 5 වප්ල්වහ න්වග්ඩ කිුමපන පාය අාක 163 දයන ස්ථානවයහි ිළහිටි

යනවේ ප්‍රවෘ කති වදපාර්තවම්න්තුවේ ිළහිටි යනවේ ප්‍රකාශ්න කාර්යාාශ්වයන්

මිල දී ගත හැක.

වමම හැන්සාඩ් වාර්තාව www.parliament.lk වවේ අඩවිවයන්

බාගත හැක.

ஹன்சொட் அறிக்மகயின் பிரதிகமள இல. 163, கிருலப்பமன வீதி, தபொல்சஹன்தகொட, தகொழும்பு 5இல் அமமந்துள்ள

அரசொங்க தகவல் திமைக்களத்தின் அரசொங்க தவளியீடுகள் அலுவலகத்தில்

பைம் தசலுத்திப் தபற்றுக்தகொள்ளலொம்.

இந்த ஹன்சொட் அறிக்மகமய www.parliament.lk எனும் இமையத்தளத்திலிருந்து

பதிவிறக்கம் தசய்ய முடியும்.
